ents: none) would STILL be returned by elementFromPoint.\n\nSo the bug is: ghost has `pointer-events-none` but that doesn\'t matter for `elementFromPoint`. The ghost div is z-[300] (very high z-index) and covers the target cell. `elementFromPoint` returns the ghost AppIcon. `closest(\'[data-itemid]\')` traverses up: AppIcon → ghost wrapper div → main container. None of these have `data-itemid`. So hoverId = null → no merge.\n\nTHE FIX: In `onMove`, instead of using `elementFromPoint` at the ghost\'s center (which is on top of the ghost itself), we need to either:\n\n1. Temporarily hide the ghost (set display:none), call elementFromPoint, then restore - too hacky\n2. Use a fixed offset point below the ghost position\n3. Use `elementsFromPoint` (plural) and skip the ghost\n4. Give the ghost a CSS class/attribute and skip it when traversing\n5. Or better: the ghost is at (x-36, y-36) to (x+36, y+36) approximately. But we\'re looking at (x, y) which is under the ghost.\n\nActually the cleanest fix: use `document.elementsFromPoint()` (plural, returns all elements at that point) and skip the ghost (which we can identify by checking it\'s not inside `containerRef` or by checking for the absence of `data-cell`).\n\nWait even simpler: the ghost element itself doesn\'t have `data-cell` or `data-itemid`. The ghost is a fixed-position div. When we call `elementFromPoint`, we get the ghost or its children. Then `closest(\'[data-itemid]\')` is called on that element. The ghost\'s children (AppIcon) also don\'t have `data-itemid`. The ghost wrapper has class containing `pointer-events-none`. \n\nBUT: `closest` also traverses UP the DOM tree. If the ghost is a direct child of the root div (which doesn\'t have `data-itemid`), then `closest(\'[data-itemid]\')` returns null. ✓ This confirms the bug.\n\nBEST FIX: Use `document.elementsFromPoint(x, y)` which returns ALL elements stacked at that point, then find the first one that has/is inside a `[data-itemid]` element:\n\n```tsx\nconst els = document.elementsFromPoint(e.clientX, e.clientY);\nlet cell: HTMLElement | null = null;\nfor (const el of els) {\n  const found = (el as HTMLElement).closest?.(\'[data-itemid]\') as HTMLElement | null;\n  if (found) { cell = found; break; }\n}\n```\n\nThis skips the ghost (which has no `data-itemid` ancestor) and finds the actual cell below.\n\nApply this fix to BOTH the `onMove` hoverId detection AND the `onUp` cell detection.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

Command: str_replace
Old String:

```
      // 用 elementsFromPoint 穿透 ghost 层（ghost z-[300] 覆盖目标，elementFromPoint 会停在它上面）
      const els = document.elementsFromPoint(e.clientX, e.clientY);

      }
```

    73 function collectIconUrls(data: DesktopData): Set<string> {
    74   const urls = new Set<string>();
    75   const addItem = (it: DesktopItem) => {
    76     if (it.iconUrl) urls.add(it.iconUrl);
    77     it.children?.forEach(addItem);
    78   };
    79   data.pages.forEach((page) => page.forEach(addItem));
    80   data.dock.forEach(addItem);
    81   return urls;
    82 }

    84 // 查找空白位置
    85 function findEmptySlot(
    86   pages: DesktopItem[][],
    87   preferPage?: number,
    88 ): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
    89   // 从 preferPage 开始搜索，保证新应用优先出现在当前页
    90   const order = preferPage !== undefined
    91     ? [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)]
    92     : Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i);
    93 
    94   for (const p of order) {
    95     for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
    96       // widget 独占整行，跳过该行所有列
    97       if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
    98       for (let c = 0; c < MAX_COLS; c++) {
    99         const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);
   100         if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
   101       }
   102     }
   103   }
   104   return null;
   105 }

   644 function findItem(

   655 // 辅助：在 preferPage 上找第一个空格（跳过被拖拽项自身），用于边缘松手时的回退落点
   656 function findFirstEmpty(
   657   pages: DesktopItem[][],
   658   preferPage: number,
   659   excludeId?: string,
   660 ): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
   661   const order = [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)];
   662   for (const p of order) {
   663     for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
   664       if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
   665       for (let c = 0; c < MAX_COLS; c++) {
   666         const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c && it.id !== excludeId);
   667         if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
   668       }
   669     }
   670   }
   671   return null;
   672 }

    63   const handlePointerDown = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    64     // 阻止默认行为，防止浏览器 context-menu / text-select / callout 干扰长按
    65     e.preventDefault();
    66     e.currentTarget.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);

    72       longFiredRef.current = true;
    73       onLongPress?.(e.clientX, e.clientY);
    74     }, LONG_PRESS_MS);
    75   }, [onLongPress]);
    76 
    77   const handlePointerMove = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    78     if (dragStartedRef.current) return;
    79     const dx = e.clientX - startXRef.current;
    80     const dy = e.clientY - startYRef.current;
    81     if (Math.hypot(dx, dy) > DRAG_THRESHOLD) {
    82       dragStartedRef.current = true;

    84       // 拖拽正式开始时立即释放指针捕获：

    86       if (e.currentTarget.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {

    91   }, [item, onDragBegin, cancelLongPress]);

Old String: ```
// 查找空白位置
function findEmptySlot(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
  preferPage?: number,
): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
  // 从 preferPage 开始搜索，保证新应用优先出现在当前页
  const order = preferPage !== undefined
    ? [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)]
    : Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i);

  for (const p of order) {
    for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
      // widget 独占整行，跳过该行所有列
      if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
      for (let c = 0; c < MAX_COLS; c++) {
        const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);
        if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}
```
New String: ```
// 查找空白位置（maxCols 限制实际渲染列数，避免图标放到不可见列）
function findEmptySlot(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
  preferPage?: number,
  maxCols: number = MAX_COLS,
): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
  // 从 preferPage 开始搜索，保证新应用优先出现在当前页
  const order = preferPage !== undefined
    ? [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)]
    : Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i);

  for (const p of order) {
    for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
      // widget 独占整行，跳过该行所有列
      if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
      for (let c = 0; c < maxCols; c++) {
        const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);
        if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}
```

```
// 辅助：在 preferPage 上找第一个空格（跳过被拖拽项自身），用于边缘松手时的回退落点
function findFirstEmpty(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
  preferPage: number,
  excludeId?: string,
): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
  const order = [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)];
  for (const p of order) {
    for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
      if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
      for (let c = 0; c < MAX_COLS; c++) {
        const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c && it.id !== excludeId);
        if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}
```
New String: ```
// 辅助：在 preferPage 上找第一个空格（跳过被拖拽项自身），用于边缘松手时的回退落点
function findFirstEmpty(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
  preferPage: number,
  excludeId?: string,
  maxCols: number = MAX_COLS,
): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
  const order = [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)];
  for (const p of order) {
    for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
      if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
      for (let c = 0; c < maxCols; c++) {
        const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c && it.id !== excludeId);
        if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}
```

    83 
    84 // 查找空白位置（maxCols 限制实际渲染列数，避免图标放到不可见列）
    85 function findEmptySlot(
    86   pages: DesktopItem[][],
    87   preferPage?: number,
    88   maxCols: number = MAX_COLS,
    89 ): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
    90   // 从 preferPage 开始搜索，保证新应用优先出现在当前页
    91   const order = preferPage !== undefined
    92     ? [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)]
    93     : Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i);
    94 
    95   for (const p of order) {
    96     for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
    97       // widget 独占整行，跳过该行所有列
    98       if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
    99       for (let c = 0; c < maxCols; c++) {
   100         const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);
   101         if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
   102       }
   103     }
   104   }
   105   return null;
   106 }

```
      // 用几何矩形检测穿透 ghost：遍历所有带 data-itemid 的格子，判断指针是否在其内
      // 比 elementsFromPoint 更可靠，不受 z-index / pointer-events 影响
      let hoverId: string | null = null;
      const itemCells = document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('[data-cell][data-itemid]');
      for (const cellEl of itemCells) {
        const r = cellEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        if (e.clientX >= r.left && e.clientX <= r.right && e.clientY >= r.top && e.clientY <= r.bottom) {
          hoverId = cellEl.dataset.itemid!;
          break;
        }
      }
      setDragOverItem(hoverId ?? null);
```

     1 import React, { useState, useRef, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
     2 import type { DesktopItem } from '@/types';
     3 import { getColorStyle } from '@/lib/colors';
     4 import { useDesktop } from '@/contexts/DesktopContext';
     5 import { Folder, Settings, RefreshCw, Globe, Plus, X } from 'lucide-react';
     6 import { getIconCache, fetchAndCacheIcon } from '@/lib/iconCache';
     7 import { getDirectFaviconUrl, normalizeUrl } from '@/lib/favicon';
     8 
     9 interface AppIconProps {
    10   item: DesktopItem;
    11   onClick?: () => void;
    12   onLongPress?: (x: number, y: number) => void;
    13   onDragBegin?: (item: DesktopItem, x: number, y: number) => void;
    14   onDeleteInEditMode?: (id: string) => void;
    15   size?: 'normal' | 'small';
    16   ghost?: boolean;
    17   /** 覆盖图标尺寸（px），不传则使用 settings.iconSize */
    18   iconPx?: number;
    19 }
    20 
    21 const LONG_PRESS_MS = 500;
    22 // 手机端手指轻微抖动约 5-10px，阈值设为 14px 以避免误触取消长按
    23 const DRAG_THRESHOLD = 14;
    24 
    25 const AppIcon: React.FC<AppIconProps> = ({
    26   item, onClick, onLongPress, onDragBegin,
    27   onDeleteInEditMode, size = 'normal', ghost = false, iconPx,
    28 }) => {
    29   const { editMode, settings } = useDesktop();
    30   const [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);
    31   const [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(false);
    32   // 优先使用本地缓存的 DataURL，无缓存时使用远程 URL
    33   const [iconSrc, setIconSrc] = useState<string | undefined>(() =>
    34     item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined
    35   );
    36 
    37   // item.iconUrl 变化时（编辑后）同步更新 iconSrc
    38   useEffect(() => {
    39     if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }
    40     setImgError(false);
    41     setImgLoaded(false);
    42     setIconSrc(getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl);
    43   }, [item.iconUrl]);
    44 
    45   const longTimerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
    46   const longFiredRef  = useRef(false);
    47   const startXRef     = useRef(0);
    48   const startYRef     = useRef(0);
    49   const dragStartedRef = useRef(false);
    50 
    51   const isSmall = size === 'small';
    52   // 图标尺寸：small 固定, normal 使用 settings 或 iconPx 覆盖
    53   const px = isSmall ? 48 : (iconPx ?? settings.iconSize ?? 46);
    54   const textSize = isSmall ? 'text-[10px]' : 'text-[11px]';
    55 
    56   // 新拟态风格阴影
    57   const isNeumorphism = settings.style === 'neumorphism';
    58 
    59   const cancelLongPress = useCallback(() => {
    60     if (longTimerRef.current) { clearTimeout(longTimerRef.current); longTimerRef.current = null; }
    61   }, []);
    62 
    63   const handlePointerDown = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    64     // 阻止默认行为，防止浏览器 context-menu / text-select / callout 干扰长按
    65     e.preventDefault();
    66     e.currentTarget.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    67     startXRef.current = e.clientX;
    68     startYRef.current = e.clientY;
    69     longFiredRef.current = false;
    70     dragStartedRef.current = false;
    71     longTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
    72       longFiredRef.current = true;
    73       onLongPress?.(e.clientX, e.clientY);
    74     }, LONG_PRESS_MS);
    75   }, [onLongPress]);
    76 
    77   const handlePointerMove = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    78     if (dragStartedRef.current) return;
    79     const dx = e.clientX - startXRef.current;
    80     const dy = e.clientY - startYRef.current;
    81     if (Math.hypot(dx, dy) > DRAG_THRESHOLD) {
    82       dragStartedRef.current = true;
    83       cancelLongPress();
    84       // 拖拽正式开始时立即释放指针捕获：
    85       // 若保留捕获，换页时 AppIcon 会从 DOM 卸载，浏览器因此触发 pointercancel 清除拖拽状态
    86       if (e.currentTarget.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
    87         e.currentTarget.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    88       }
    89       onDragBegin?.(item, e.clientX, e.clientY);
    90     }
    91   }, [item, onDragBegin, cancelLongPress]);
    92 
    93   const handlePointerUp = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    94     dragStartedRef.current = false;
    95     cancelLongPress();
    96     // 确保释放捕获（未达到拖拽阈值时）
    97     if (e.currentTarget.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
    98       e.currentTarget.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    99     }
   100   }, [cancelLongPress]);
   101 
   102   const handleClick = useCallback(() => {
   103     if (longFiredRef.current || dragStartedRef.current) return;
   104     if (editMode && item.type !== 'system') return;
   105     if (item.type === 'app' && item.url) window.open(item.url, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer');
   106     else onClick?.();
   107   }, [editMode, item, onClick]);
   108 
   109   const iconStyle: React.CSSProperties = {
   110     width: px, height: px,
   111     borderRadius: '22%',
   112     flexShrink: 0,
   113     ...(isNeumorphism ? {
   114       boxShadow: '4px 4px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.12), -4px -4px 10px rgba(255,255,255,0.7)',
   115     } : {}),
   116   };
   117 
   118   const renderIconContent = () => {
   119     if (item.type === 'system') {
   120       const iconMap: Record<string, React.ElementType> = {
   121         'sys-settings': Settings, 'sys-sync': RefreshCw, 'sys-add': Plus,
   122       };
   123       const Icon = iconMap[item.id] ?? Globe;
   124       return (
   125         <div className="flex items-center justify-center ios-icon-shadow transition-transform duration-200"
   126           style={{ ...iconStyle, background: getColorStyle(item.color) }}>
   127           <Icon style={{ width: px * 0.5, height: px * 0.5 }} className="text-white" strokeWidth={2} />
   128         </div>
   129       );
   130     }
   131     if (item.type === 'folder') {
   132       // 取前 4 个子项，以 2×2 网格展示缩略图
   133       const preview = (item.children || []).slice(0, 4);
   134       const isNeu = settings.style === 'neumorphism';
   135       // 单个格子边长（去掉间距后均分）
   136       const cellPx = (px * 0.68 - 4) / 2; // gap=4px，共 1 条
   137       return (
   138         <div
   139           className="ios-icon-shadow overflow-hidden flex items-center justify-center"
   140           style={{
   141             ...iconStyle,
   142             background: isNeu ? 'rgba(232,237,245,0.55)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)',
   143             backdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   144             WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   145 
   146           }}
   147         >
   148           {preview.length > 0 ? (
   149             <div
   150               className="grid gap-[4px]"
   151               style={{
   152                 gridTemplateColumns: `repeat(2, ${cellPx}px)`,
   153                 gridTemplateRows: `repeat(2, ${cellPx}px)`,
   154               }}
   155             >
   156               {preview.map((child) => (
   157                 <div
   158                   key={child.id}
   159                   className="rounded-[18%] overflow-hidden flex items-center justify-center"
   160                   style={{
   161                     width: cellPx,
   162                     height: cellPx,
   163                     background: child.iconUrl ? 'transparent' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)',
   164                     flexShrink: 0,
   165                   }}
   166                 >
   167                   {child.iconUrl ? (
   168                     <img
   169                       src={getIconCache(child.iconUrl) ?? child.iconUrl}
   170                       alt=""
   171                       draggable={false}
   172                       style={{ width: cellPx, height: cellPx, objectFit: 'cover', display: 'block' }}
   173                     />
   174                   ) : (
   175                     <span className="text-white font-bold drop-shadow" style={{ fontSize: px * 0.16 }}>
   176                       {child.name.slice(0, 1)}
   177                     </span>
   178                   )}
   179                 </div>
   180               ))}
   181             </div>
   182           ) : (
   183             <Folder style={{ width: px * 0.5, height: px * 0.5 }} className="text-white drop-shadow" />
   184           )}
   185         </div>
   186       );
   187     }
   188     if (iconSrc && !imgError) {
   189       return (
   190         <div
   191           className="overflow-hidden ios-icon-shadow relative"
   192           style={{
   193             ...iconStyle,
   194             background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)',
   195             backdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   196             WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   197 
   198           }}
   199         >
   200           {/* 骨架屏：图片加载完成前显示 shimmer 动画 */}
   201           {!imgLoaded && (
   202             <div
   203               className="absolute inset-0 animate-skeleton-pulse"
   204               style={{ borderRadius: '22%', background: 'linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(200,200,200,0.3) 25%,rgba(220,220,220,0.5) 50%,rgba(200,200,200,0.3) 75%)', backgroundSize: '200% 100%' }}
   205             />
   206           )}
   207           <img
   208             src={iconSrc}
   209             alt={item.name}
   210             draggable={false}
   211             className="w-full h-full object-cover"
   212             style={{ opacity: imgLoaded ? 1 : 0, transition: 'opacity 0.2s ease' }}
   213             onLoad={() => {
   214               setImgLoaded(true);
   215               // 图片加载成功后，后台静默缓存为 DataURL；不修改 iconSrc 避免 src 变动闪白
   216               if (!item.iconUrl || iconSrc.startsWith('data:')) return;
   217               fetchAndCacheIcon(item.iconUrl); // fire-and-forget，下次挂载时从缓存读取
   218             }}
   219             onError={(e) => {
   220               const img = e.currentTarget;
   221               // 尝试直连 favicon.ico 作为回退
   222               if (item.url && !img.dataset.fallbackTried) {
   223                 img.dataset.fallbackTried = '1';
   224                 const fallback = getDirectFaviconUrl(normalizeUrl(item.url));
   225                 if (fallback && fallback !== iconSrc) { img.src = fallback; return; }
   226               }
   227               setImgError(true);
   228             }}
   229           />
   230         </div>
   231       );
   232     }
   233     return (
   234       <div
   235         className="flex items-center justify-center ios-icon-shadow"
   236         style={{
   237           ...iconStyle,
   238           background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)',
   239           backdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   240           WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   241 
   242         }}
   243       >
   244         {item.url ? (
   245           <Globe style={{ width: px * 0.5, height: px * 0.5 }} className="text-white drop-shadow" />
   246         ) : (
   247           <span className="text-white font-bold uppercase drop-shadow" style={{ fontSize: px * 0.35 }}>{item.name.slice(0, 1)}</span>
   248         )}
   249       </div>
   250     );
   251   };
   252 
   253   return (
   254     <div className={`relative ${ghost ? 'opacity-40' : ''}`}>
   255       <button
   256         type="button"
   257         onClick={handleClick}
   258         onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
   259         onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
   260         onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
   261         onPointerCancel={handlePointerUp}
   262         onContextMenu={(e) => e.preventDefault()}
   263         className={`flex flex-col items-center gap-1 select-none touch-none ${editMode ? 'animate-wiggle' : ''} transition-transform active:scale-95`}
   264       >
   265         {renderIconContent()}
   266         <span
   267           className={`app-icon-label ${textSize} font-medium truncate ${isNeumorphism ? 'text-slate-600' : 'text-white drop-shadow-md'}`}
   268           style={{ maxWidth: px + 8 }}
   269         >
   270           {item.name}
   271         </span>
   272       </button>
   273       {editMode && item.type !== 'system' && onDeleteInEditMode && (
   274         <button
   275           type="button"
   276           onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onDeleteInEditMode(item.id); }}
   277           className="absolute -top-1 -left-1 z-20 w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-destructive flex items-center justify-center shadow-md"
   278           aria-label="删除"
   279         >
   280           <X className="w-3 h-3 text-white" strokeWidth={3} />
   281         </button>
   282       )}
   283     </div>
   284   );
   285 };
   286 
   287 export default AppIcon;

AgentThinkAction(thought='Now I understand the issue clearly. Looking at AppIcon.tsx:\n\nLine 30-35:\n```tsx\nconst [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);\nconst [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(false);\nconst [iconSrc, setIconSrc] = useState<string | undefined>(() =>\n  item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined\n);\n```\n\nThe problem is:\n1. `imgLoaded` starts as `false` \n2. The image has `opacity: imgLoaded ? 1 : 0` → starts invisible\n3. Until `onLoad` fires (which happens when the image finishes loading), the icon shows the skeleton shimmer\n\nBut here\'s the KEY ISSUE: every time `AppIcon` is **REMOUNTED** (which happens when:\n- Changing pages (items unmount/remount)\n- After drag/drop (data change causes re-render)\n\n...the component remounts with `imgLoaded = false` again. Even if the image is ALREADY LOADED by the browser (cached in HTTP cache), the component doesn\'t know this because React state is reset.\n\nWhen the component mounts:\n1. `imgLoaded = false` → image `opacity: 0`\n2. Browser immediately loads from HTTP cache\n3. `onLoad` fires → `imgLoaded = true` → opacity: 1\n\nBut there\'s a potential issue: if the browser already has the image in cache, `onLoad` fires synchronously (or very quickly), BUT React state update is async. So there\'s a brief moment where `imgLoaded = false`.\n\nActually, the more important issue: `iconSrc` is initialized as:\n```tsx\n() => item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined\n```\n\n`getIconCache(item.iconUrl)` returns the DataURL if cached. If cached as DataURL, `iconSrc` is a data: URL. When the `<img>` receives a data: URL, `onLoad` fires synchronously in some browsers, but React schedules the state update. This causes a flash.\n\nAlso, for DataURL src: `fetchAndCacheIcon` is only called after `onLoad`. The FIRST render always has `imgLoaded=false`. The `onLoad` event then fires and `setImgLoaded(true)` is called. This causes a re-render with `opacity: 1`.\n\nThe REAL FIX: We should initialize `imgLoaded` to `true` if the icon is ALREADY in the cache (as a DataURL), so no skeleton/opacity flash happens.\n\n```tsx\nconst [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) return false;\n  const cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl);\n  return cached != null; // If we have a data: URL cached, image is "already loaded"\n});\n```\n\nAdditionally, when `iconSrc` changes (in the `useEffect` for `item.iconUrl` change), we should check if the new URL is cached:\n\n```tsx\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }\n  setImgError(false);\n  const cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl);\n  if (cached) {\n    setIconSrc(cached);\n    setImgLoaded(true); // Already have it cached, no delay\n  } else {\n    setImgLoaded(false);\n    setIconSrc(item.iconUrl);\n  }\n}, [item.iconUrl]);\n```\n\nBut there\'s STILL the issue of the FIRST render on remount. Even with the init state fix, the component remounts and `useState(() => ...)` DOES initialize correctly. So if the cache has the DataURL, `imgLoaded` starts as `true`. This would fix the flash.\n\nHOWEVER: there\'s another issue. After `fetchAndCacheIcon` stores the DataURL in the cache, the NEXT time the component mounts, `getIconCache` returns the DataURL. So `imgLoaded` initializes to `true`. The image starts with `opacity: 1`. No delay!\n\nBut the FIRST time the component mounts (before `fetchAndCacheIcon` has run), `getIconCache` returns `null`, so `imgLoaded = false`. The `onLoad` fires, `setImgLoaded(true)`.\n\nFor SUBSEQUENT mounts (after page switch / after drag), `getIconCache` returns the cached DataURL, and `imgLoaded = true` from the start. But `iconSrc` is also the DataURL. So the image is shown immediately!\n\nWait, but there\'s a subtlety: when `iconSrc` is a DataURL, the `<img src={dataUrl}>` is set, and `onLoad` fires after the component renders. Before `onLoad` fires, the image has `opacity: 0` (since `imgLoaded = false` on initial state).\n\nWith my fix: `imgLoaded` starts as `true` if cached. So `opacity: 1` from the start. And `iconSrc` is the DataURL. The image displays immediately! ✓\n\nThis fixes the delay for cached icons.\n\nBUT: what about the `useEffect` that runs on mount (line 38-43)?\n\n```tsx\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }\n  setImgError(false);\n  setImgLoaded(false); // ← THIS RESETS imgLoaded to false!\n  setIconSrc(getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl);\n}, [item.iconUrl]);\n```\n\nThis `useEffect` runs after mount AND whenever `item.iconUrl` changes. On INITIAL MOUNT, `item.iconUrl` matches the initial state, so this effect runs and resets `imgLoaded = false`!\n\nThis is the ROOT CAUSE of the delay: even if `imgLoaded` was initialized to `true`, the `useEffect` on mount immediately resets it to `false`.\n\nThe fix: the `useEffect` should only run when `item.iconUrl` CHANGES (not on initial mount). Or better: it should only reset `imgLoaded` if the URL actually changed.\n\nFIX APPROACH:\n1. Initialize `imgLoaded` to `true` if icon is cached\n2. Use `useRef` to track previous `item.iconUrl` and only reset if it actually changed\n3. Don\'t run the effect on mount if the URL is the same as initial\n\nBetter approach:\n```tsx\nconst prevIconUrlRef = useRef(item.iconUrl);\n\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (item.iconUrl === prevIconUrlRef.current && prevIconUrlRef.current !== undefined) return; // Skip if unchanged\n  // Actually this doesn\'t work for mount...\n```\n\nActually the simplest fix: move the `useEffect` logic to use a `useRef` to skip the first mount:\n\n```tsx\nconst initialMountRef = useRef(true);\n\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (initialMountRef.current) {\n    initialMountRef.current = false;\n    return; // Skip initial mount - state already initialized correctly\n  }\n  // Only reset on actual URL change\n  if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }\n  setImgError(false);\n  const cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl);\n  setImgLoaded(cached != null); // true if cached, false if not\n  setIconSrc(cached ?? item.iconUrl);\n}, [item.iconUrl]);\n```\n\nThis way:\n- On initial mount: skip the effect, keep initialized state (which already checked cache)\n- On URL change: reset + check cache\n\nCombined with initializing `imgLoaded` from cache:\n```tsx\nconst [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) return false;\n  return getIconCache(item.iconUrl) != null;\n});\n```\n\nThis should fix the delay!\n\nActually, wait. Component mounts: `imgLoaded = true` (if cached) ← good\n2. The useEffect is resetting imgLoaded to false even though we just checked the cache.\n\nWith my fix using `initialMountRef`:\n1. Component mounts: `imgLoaded = true` (if cached)\n2. NO FLASH ✓\n\nThen if `item.iconUrl` changes (user edits the item):\n5. useEffect runs: not initial mount → reset imgLoaded based on cache check ✓\n\nThis is the correct fix!\n\nLet me also think about whether there\'s any other source of delay:\n\nThe `iconSrc` state is initialized from:\n```tsx\n() => item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined\n```\n\nIf `getIconCache` returns a DataURL, `iconSrc = dataUrl`. Good.\nIf `getIconCache` returns null, `iconSrc = item.iconUrl` (remote URL). Need to load. Thought: 根因找到：`AppIcon` 每次重新挂载（翻页/拖拽后数据变化导致 unmount→remount）时，`imgLoaded` 初始化为 `false`，且 `useEffect` 无论是否是初次挂载都会再次 `setImgLoaded(false)` 覆盖缓存状态 → 即使图片已有 DataURL 缓存，也要等 `onLoad` 再次触发才变回可见。

**两处并行修复：**
1. `imgLoaded` 初始化时直接检查缓存（有缓存 → `true`，跳过骨架屏）
2. `useEffect` 首次挂载跳过重置（用 `initialMountRef` 标记），只在 `iconUrl` **变化**时才重新加载
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
  const [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);
  const [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(false);
  // 优先使用本地缓存的 DataURL，无缓存时使用远程 URL
  const [iconSrc, setIconSrc] = useState<string | undefined>(() =>
    item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined
  );

  // item.iconUrl 变化时（编辑后）同步更新 iconSrc
```

```
  const [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);
  // 有本地缓存（DataURL）时直接标记已加载，避免重新挂载时闪白
  const [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(() =>
    !!(item.iconUrl && getIconCache(item.iconUrl)),
  );
  // 优先使用本地缓存的 DataURL，无缓存时使用远程 URL
  const [iconSrc, setIconSrc] = useState<string | undefined>(() =>
    item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined
  );

  // 标记是否为初次挂载：初次挂载时 state 已由 lazy initializer 正确初始化，不需要再重置
  const initialMountRef = useRef(true);

  // item.iconUrl 变化时（编辑后）同步更新 iconSrc；初次挂载跳过，避免清空缓存命中状态
  useEffect(() => {
    if (initialMountRef.current) { initialMountRef.current = false; return; }
    if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }
    setImgError(false);
    const cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl);
    setImgLoaded(cached != null); // 缓存命中 → 直接标记已加载，不等 onLoad
    setIconSrc(cached ?? item.iconUrl);
  }, [item.iconUrl]);
```
